<!-- MATURITY -->
<div id="matview">
  <div class="matwrap">
    <h2>Research readiness maturity model</h2>
    <p class="lead">Five stages an organization moves through, read across five tracks. An org's overall level is roughly the lowest stage it has reliably reached across the tracks, because you cannot share data responsibly without governance beneath it. Click any cell for its questions and the support that moves an org forward.</p>
    <a class="btn" href="../self-assessment.html">Take the self-assessment →</a>
    <div class="stages5" id="stages5"></div>
    <div class="matgrid" id="matgrid"></div>
    <p class="foot" style="padding-left:0">This model replaces the earlier status tiers. The tiers described observable infrastructure; this model describes an organization's own trajectory and is populated by self-assessment, not assigned from outside.</p>
  </div>
</div>

Producing data with intent."},{"id":5,"name":"Data Sharing","blurb":"Contributing standardized, documented data or metadata to shared or open resources for use beyond the org."}],"composite_rule":"An org's composite level is roughly the lowest stage it has reliably reached across the core tracks. You cannot be Data Sharing overall if you have no governance. The tracks show exactly where an org is ahead or behind.","tracks":[{"id":"foundation","name":"Organizational Foundation","stages":[{"s":1,"label":"Informal community","q":["Do we have a space where patients and families find each other?","Does someone informally keep things going?"],"needs":"Turning a loose group into something durable; understanding what becoming an organization involves.","help":["Plain language orientation on nonprofit formation","Connect founders to peer organizations who have made the leap"]},{"s":2,"label":"Unincorporated association","q":["Do we have identified leaders, even without legal status?","Do we have a shared mission written down?"],"needs":"The legal and administrative mechanics of incorporation; drafting governing documents.","help":["Pro bono legal services for incorporation and bylaws","Governance templates","Board recruitment guidance"]},{"s":3,"label":"Incorporated nonprofit","q":["Are we a registered nonprofit with bylaws and a functioning board?","Can we legally accept donations and enter agreements?"],"needs":"Moving from legally exists to actually operating; first strategic plan; early fundraising.","help":["Strategic planning facilitation","Grant writing support","Nonprofit financial and accounting services"]},{"s":4,"label":"Staffed and resourced","q":["Do we have paid staff or a dedicated contractor?","Do we have a strategic plan and a research budget line?"],"needs":"Building research capacity; hiring the right roles; sustainable funding.","help":["Research operations consulting","Advice on hiring a research lead","Introductions to research funders"]},{"s":5,"label":"Sustainable","q":["Do we have diversified funding and someone leading research?","Could the org survive its founder's departure?"],"needs":"Succession, long term sustainability, scaling impact.","help":["Executive coaching and succession planning","Endowment or reserve building strategy","Governance maturity review"]}]},{"id":"engagement","name":"Scientific and Community Engagement","stages":[{"s":1,"label":"Peer support","q":["Do members share experiences and information?"],"needs":"Recognizing the community's value as a research asset.","help":["Educate the community on how patient experience informs research","Introduce the concept of patient reported data"]},{"s":2,"label":"Awareness and connecting","q":["Do we help families find clinicians or trials?","Do we do awareness raising beyond our members?"],"needs":"Identifying which clinicians and researchers work on their condition.","help":["Clinician and researcher landscape mapping","Trial finder navigation support"]},{"s":3,"label":"Priorities from community","q":["Have we asked our community what research is important to them?","Do we have a group that channels patient input into priorities?"],"needs":"Running a credible priority setting process.","help":["Facilitate a research priority setting exercise (James Lind Alliance style)","Survey design"]},{"s":4,"label":"Advisory board","q":["Do we have a scientific or medical advisory board that meets and influences decisions?"],"needs":"Recruiting credible experts; running an effective board.","help":["Serve on or help recruit the advisory board","Advise on charters and conflict of interest policy"]},{"s":5,"label":"Agenda setting","q":["Do we help define the research agenda for our condition?","Have researchers co-designed studies with us?"],"needs":"Sustaining genuine co-design as the org scales.","help":["Partner as a co-investigator","Build patient engagement into grant proposals as a named partner"]}]},{"id":"ecosystem","name":"Ecosystem Integration","stages":[{"s":1,"label":"Isolated","q":["Are we essentially working on our own?"],"needs":"Knowing the ecosystem exists and how to enter it.","help":["Introductions to consortia and umbrella organizations","An ecosystem map"]},{"s":2,"label":"Informal ties","q":["Do we have a relationship with at least one researcher or clinician?"],"needs":"Converting a single relationship into broader engagement.","help":["Warm introductions to relevant consortia (REN, CombinedBrain, NORD)"]},{"s":3,"label":"Consortium member","q":["Are we an active member of a consortium or umbrella?"],"needs":"Getting real value from membership, not just belonging.","help":["Advise on how to participate actively","Identify collaboration opportunities within the consortium"]},{"s":4,"label":"Active collaborations","q":["Are we in shared projects with other organizations?"],"needs":"Managing multi party projects and data sharing across orgs.","help":["Project management support","Multi site agreement and data governance templates"]},{"s":5,"label":"Recognized node","q":["Do others come to us as a partner or convener?"],"needs":"The load of convening; staying strategic.","help":["Infrastructure or staffing to support a convening role","Co-host workshops"]}]},{"id":"data","name":"Data Infrastructure","stages":[{"s":1,"label":"No structured data","q":["Is most of what we know anecdotal or scattered?"],"needs":"Understanding what structured data is and its importance.","help":["A plain language primer on registries","Help define what data would be worth collecting"]},{"s":2,"label":"Contact registry","q":["Do we have a maintained list of who our patients are and how to reach them?"],"needs":"Moving from a contact list to research data; privacy basics.","help":["Advise on consent for re-contact","Help select a registry platform if they decide they want that"]},{"s":3,"label":"Patient reported registry","q":["Do we collect structured patient reported data on a real platform, with meaningful enrollment?"],"needs":"Survey and instrument quality; boosting enrollment and retention.","help":["Instrument design and validation","Recruitment strategy","Biostatistics consultation"]},{"s":4,"label":"Natural history and longitudinal","q":["Are we collecting data over time with a defined data model?"],"needs":"Clinical data collection, longitudinal follow up, data quality.","help":["Natural history study design","Clinical data management","REDCap or equivalent setup"]},{"s":5,"label":"Harmonized to standards","q":["Is our data mapped to common standards and combinable with other datasets?"],"needs":"Mapping to common data elements; interoperability.","help":["Data harmonization services","Ontology and common data element mapping","Informatics support"]}]},{"id":"governance","name":"Data Governance and Sharing","north_star":true,"stages":[{"s":1,"label":"No governance","q":["Are we holding data without a clear consent or privacy framework?"],"needs":"Basic consent, privacy, and ethics; understanding obligations.","help":["Draft research consent and privacy policies","IRB and ethics navigation"]},{"s":2,"label":"Internal governance","q":["Do we have consent and privacy policies, with data held internally?"],"needs":"Preparing data to be intelligible and shareable beyond the org.","help":["Review consent for whether it permits future sharing","Introduce data sharing concepts"]},{"s":3,"label":"Documented and standardized","q":["Do we have a published data dictionary and standardized variables?","Could an outsider understand our dataset from the documentation alone?"],"needs":"Writing and publishing a data dictionary; standardizing variables.","help":["Build the data dictionary","Map variables to common data elements","Documentation support"]},{"s":4,"label":"Shared with a partner","q":["Have we shared data with a vetted partner under a formal agreement (Data for the Common Good, RDCA-DAP)?","Do we have a governance policy for how sharing decisions get made?"],"needs":"Data sharing agreements; a governance process for access requests.","help":["Draft data sharing and use agreements","Set up a data access committee","Broker partner relationships"]},{"s":5,"label":"Open and broadly accessible","q":["Is our data or metadata findable by researchers beyond named partners, meeting FAIR principles?","Can qualified researchers discover and request it through a defined process?"],"needs":"Making data FAIR; sustaining open access responsibly.","help":["FAIR-ification services","Deposit into recognized repositories","Publish discoverable metadata even when raw data stays controlled"]}]}]};
const byGene={}; DATA.forEach(g=>byGene[g.gene]=g);
const SC={1:'var(--s1)',2:'var(--s2)',3:'var(--s3)',4:'var(--s4)',5:'var(--s5)'};
function esc(s){return (s||'').replace(/[&<>"]/g,c=>({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;'}[c]))}

/* ---------- view switch ---------- */
function setView(v){
  document.querySelectorAll('.viewtabs button').forEach(b=>b.classList.toggle('on',b.dataset.v===v));
  document.getElementById('refview').style.display=v==='ref'?'grid':'none';
  document.getElementById('netview').classList.toggle('show',v==='net');
  document.getElementById('matview').classList.toggle('show',v==='mat');
  if(v==='net'){sizeCanvas(); if(!net.started){browseCommunity(topComs[0].id);} }
}

/* ---------- reference list ---------- */
const list=document.getElementById('list');
function renderList(f=''){
  f=f.trim().toUpperCase(); list.innerHTML='';
  DATA.filter(g=>!f||g.gene.toUpperCase().includes(f)).forEach(g=>{
    const el=document.createElement('div'); el.className='row'; el.dataset.gene=g.gene;
    el.innerHTML=`<span class="ind" style="background:${SC[g.ind.lvl]}" title="Indicative infrastructure level">${g.ind.lvl}</span>
      <span class="nm">${g.gene}</span>
      <span class="mt"><b class="lensdot ${g.in_registry?'on':''}">R</b><b class="lensdot net ${g.in_network?'on':''}">N</b></span>`;
    el.onclick=()=>selectGene(g.gene); list.appendChild(el);
  });
}
function refLinks(g){
  return [['PubMed',g.pubmed_url],['OMIM',g.omim_url],['HGNC',g.hgnc_url],['NCBI',g.ncbi_url],['ClinVar',g.clinvar_url],['gnomAD',g.gnomad_url],['GeneReviews',g.genereviews_url],['Orphanet',g.orphanet_gene_url],['ClinicalTrials',g.clinicaltrials_url]]
   .filter(x=>x[1]).map(x=>`<a class="reflink" target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="${esc(x[1])}">${x[0]} ↗</a>`).join('');
}
function infraItem(k,label,url){
  if(!k) return `<div class="item"><span class="k">${label}</span><span class="none">not recorded</span></div>`;
  const v=url?`<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="${esc(url)}">${esc(k)} ↗</a>`:esc(k);
  return `<div class="item"><span class="k">${label}</span><span>${v}</span></div>`;
}
function selectGene(gene){
  const g=byGene[gene]; if(!g)return;
  [...list.children].forEach(c=>c.classList.toggle('on',c.dataset.gene===gene));
  const i=g.ind;
  const segs=[1,2,3,4,5].map(n=>`<div class="seg" style="background:${n<=i.lvl?SC[i.lvl]:'var(--line)'}"></div>`).join('');
  const platforms=(g.platforms_list&&g.platforms_list.length)?g.platforms_list.map(p=>`<a class="chip" target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="${esc(p.url)}">${esc(p.label)} ↗</a>`).join(''):(g.platforms_text?`<span class="chip">${esc(g.platforms_text)}</span>`:'<span class="none">none recorded</span>');
  const socials=[['LinkedIn',g.linkedin],['Facebook',g.facebook],['Instagram',g.instagram],['YouTube',g.youtube],['X',g.twitter]].filter(s=>s[1]).map(s=>`<a class="chip gold" target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="${esc(s[1])}">${s[0]} ↗</a>`).join('');
  const pagChips=g.net_pags.length?g.net_pags.map(p=>`<span class="chip teal">${esc(p)}</span>`).join(''):'<span class="none">No advocacy organizations linked in the network layer.</span>';
  const disChips=g.net_diseases.length?`<div class="chiprow">${g.net_diseases.map(d=>`<span class="chip grn">${esc(d)}</span>`).join('')}</div>`:'<div class="none" style="font-size:13px">No related conditions surface through shared organizations.</div>';
  let netnote = !g.in_network
    ? 'This gene has a full reference card but is not in the network layer yet. The relationship data cover 173 genes; widening that set is a defined next step, not a redesign, because the join key already exists.'
    : (g.net_pags.length===0 ? 'Named in the network but with no advocacy links yet, it sits at the edge of the graph.'
      : (g.net_diseases.length===0 ? `Connected to ${g.net_pags.length} organization${g.net_pags.length>1?'s':''}, with no sibling conditions sharing them. A focused, single-condition community.`
        : `Shares advocacy infrastructure with ${g.net_diseases.length} related condition${g.net_diseases.length>1?'s':''} through ${g.net_pags.length} organization${g.net_pags.length>1?'s':''}. The overlap is where coordination is already happening.`));
  document.getElementById('refstage').innerHTML=`
   <div class="ghead">
     <h2>${g.gene}</h2>
     <div class="sub">${esc(g.disorder||g.phenotype||'Monogenic epilepsy gene')}${g.inheritance?' · '+esc(g.inheritance):''}${g.omim_gene?' · OMIM '+esc(g.omim_gene):''}</div>
     <div class="indstrip">${segs}<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--muted)">Indicative infrastructure, from observable signals. Authoritative level comes from <a href="../self-assessment.html">self-assessment</a>.</span></div>
   </div>
   <div class="cols">
     <section class="lens left">
       <div class="lh"><span class="ic">R</span><h3>Reference lens</h3></div>
       <div class="lhsub">Depth on one gene at a time.</div>
       <div class="field"><div class="flabel">Identifiers</div><div class="idgrid">
         <div><span class="mono">HGNC</span> ${esc(g.hgnc||'—')}</div><div><span class="mono">Entrez</span> ${esc(g.entrez||'—')}</div>
         <div><span class="mono">Ensembl</span> ${esc(g.ensembl||'—')}</div><div><span class="mono">OMIM</span> ${esc(g.omim_gene||'—')}</div></div></div>
       <div class="field"><div class="flabel">Inheritance and phenotype</div><div>${esc(g.inheritance||'—')} · ${esc(g.phenotype||'—')}</div></div>
       <hr class="soft">
       <div class="field"><div class="flabel">Community infrastructure</div><div class="infra">
         ${infraItem(g.foundation,'Foundation',g.foundation_url)}${infraItem(g.registry,'Registry',g.registry_url)}
         ${infraItem(g.ssl,'Searchlight','')}${infraItem(g.cords,'CoRDS','')}
         ${infraItem(g.therapeutics,'Therapeutics','')}${infraItem(g.fda_report,'FDA PFDD',g.fda_report_url)}</div></div>
       <div class="field"><div class="flabel">Platforms</div><div class="chiprow">${platforms}</div></div>
       ${socials?`<div class="field"><div class="flabel">Channels</div><div class="chiprow">${socials}</div></div>`:''}
       <hr class="soft">
       <div class="field"><div class="flabel">Canonical references</div><div class="reflinks">${refLinks(g)}</div></div>
     </section>
     <section class="lens right">
       <div class="lh"><span class="ic">N</span><h3>Network lens</h3></div>
       <div class="lhsub">This gene's place among conditions and organizations.</div>
       ${g.in_network?`
       <div class="netstat">
         <div><div class="n">${g.net_pags.length}</div><div class="l">Advocacy orgs</div></div>
         <div><div class="n">${g.net_diseases.length}</div><div class="l">Related conditions</div></div>
         <div><div class="n">${g.degree}</div><div class="l">Direct links</div></div></div>
       <div class="cbadge">◆ Community ${g.community}</div>
       <div class="note" style="margin-top:14px">${netnote}</div>
       <div class="field"><div class="flabel">Advocacy organizations</div><div class="chiprow">${pagChips}</div></div>
       <div class="field"><div class="flabel">Conditions sharing those organizations</div>${disChips}</div>
       <button class="btn ghost" onclick="setView('net');centerNode('${esc(g.gene)}')">Open in network →</button>`
       :`<div class="note">${netnote}</div>`}
     </section>
   </div>
   <div class="foot">Reference lens: Genetic Epilepsy Landscape (Genes4Epilepsy v2026-03). Network lens: Monogenic Epilepsy Landscape Atlas. Joined on gene symbol.</div>`;
  document.getElementById('refstage').scrollTop=0;
}
document.getElementById('q').addEventListener('input',e=>renderList(e.target.value));
renderList();

/* ---------- NETWORK (canvas force, ego + community) ---------- */
const cv=document.getElementById('cv'),ctx=cv.getContext('2d'),tip=document.getElementById('tip');
const NID={}; GRAPH.nodes.forEach(n=>NID[n.id]=n);
const NAME={}; GRAPH.nodes.forEach(n=>NAME[n.name.toLowerCase()]=n);
const ADJ={}; GRAPH.nodes.forEach(n=>ADJ[n.id]=[]);
GRAPH.links.forEach(([a,b])=>{if(ADJ[a]&&ADJ[b]){ADJ[a].push(b);ADJ[b].push(a);}});
const COM={}; GRAPH.nodes.forEach(n=>{(COM[n.c]=COM[n.c]||[]).push(n.id)});
const topComs=Object.entries(COM).map(([id,m])=>({id:+id,size:m.length})).filter(c=>c.size>=5).sort((a,b)=>b.size-a.size).slice(0,12);
const COMC=['#6d28d9','#155f83','#b4892b','#1f6b4f','#c2410c','#7c3aed','#0e7490','#9d174d','#4d7c0f','#b45309','#1d4ed8','#a21caf'];
let net={started:false,nodes:[],links:[],tx:0,ty:0,scale:1,drag:null};

function shapeFor(t){return t}
function buildSub(ids){
  const set=new Set(ids); const ns=[...set].map(id=>NID[id]).filter(Boolean);
  const ls=GRAPH.links.filter(([a,b])=>set.has(a)&&set.has(b));
  const cx=cv.width/2,cy=cv.height/2;
  net.nodes=ns.map((n,i)=>({...n,x:cx+Math.cos(i/ns.length*6.28)*180+(Math.random()*40-20),y:cy+Math.sin(i/ns.length*6.28)*180+(Math.random()*40-20),vx:0,vy:0,r:n.t==='g'?7:n.t==='d'?6:5}));
  const pos={}; net.nodes.forEach(n=>pos[n.id]=n);
  net.links=ls.map(([a,b])=>({a:pos[a],b:pos[b]})).filter(l=>l.a&&l.b);
  net.started=true; net.tx=0;net.ty=0;net.scale=1;
  document.getElementById('nhint').style.display=net.nodes.length>2?'none':'block';
}
function centerNode(name){
  const n=NAME[(name||'').toLowerCase()]; if(!n){return;}
  const ids=[n.id,...ADJ[n.id]];
  // add 2-hop for genes (gene->pag->disease) capped
  let extra=[]; ADJ[n.id].forEach(p=>{ADJ[p].slice(0,14).forEach(x=>extra.push(x))});
  buildSub([...new Set([...ids,...extra])].slice(0,160));
  net.focus=n.id;
}
function browseCommunity(cid){ buildSub(COM[cid].slice(0,170)); net.focus=null;
  document.querySelectorAll('.comitem').forEach(e=>e.classList.toggle('on',+e.dataset.c===cid)); }
function sizeCanvas(){const r=cv.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();cv.width=r.width;cv.height=r.height;}
window.addEventListener('resize',()=>{sizeCanvas();});

function tick(){
  if(document.getElementById('netview').classList.contains('show')&&net.nodes.length){
    const N=net.nodes;
    for(let i=0;i<N.length;i++){const a=N[i];
      for(let j=i+1;j<N.length;j++){const b=N[j];let dx=a.x-b.x,dy=a.y-b.y,d2=dx*dx+dy*dy||1;
        if(d2<40000){const f=900/d2;const d=Math.sqrt(d2);a.vx+=dx/d*f;a.vy+=dy/d*f;b.vx-=dx/d*f;b.vy-=dy/d*f;}}}
    net.links.forEach(l=>{let dx=l.b.x-l.a.x,dy=l.b.y-l.a.y,d=Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy)||1,f=(d-70)*0.012;
      l.a.vx+=dx/d*f;l.a.vy+=dy/d*f;l.b.vx-=dx/d*f;l.b.vy-=dy/d*f;});
    const cx=cv.width/2,cy=cv.height/2;
    N.forEach(n=>{n.vx+=(cx-n.x)*0.002;n.vy+=(cy-n.y)*0.002;n.vx*=.86;n.vy*=.86;
      if(n!==net.dragn){n.x+=n.vx;n.y+=n.vy;}});
    draw();
  }
  requestAnimationFrame(tick);
}
function draw(){
  ctx.clearRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);
  ctx.save();ctx.translate(net.tx,net.ty);ctx.scale(net.scale,net.scale);
  ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(80,70,110,.22)';
  net.links.forEach(l=>{ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(l.a.x,l.a.y);ctx.lineTo(l.b.x,l.b.y);ctx.stroke();});
  net.nodes.forEach(n=>{
    const col=COMC[n.c%COMC.length];
    ctx.fillStyle=col;ctx.strokeStyle=n.id===net.focus?'#0e1a2b':'rgba(255,255,255,.85)';ctx.lineWidth=n.id===net.focus?2.5:1;
    ctx.beginPath();
    if(n.t==='g'){ctx.arc(n.x,n.y,n.r,0,6.2832);}
    else if(n.t==='d'){ctx.rect(n.x-n.r,n.y-n.r,n.r*2,n.r*2);}
    else{ctx.moveTo(n.x,n.y-n.r);ctx.lineTo(n.x+n.r,n.y+n.r);ctx.lineTo(n.x-n.r,n.y+n.r);ctx.closePath();}
    ctx.fill();ctx.stroke();
    if(n.id===net.focus||net.scale>1.4){ctx.fillStyle='#0e1a2b';ctx.font='11px Public Sans, sans-serif';ctx.fillText(n.name,n.x+n.r+3,n.y+3);}
  });
  ctx.restore();
}
// interaction
function toWorld(mx,my){return {x:(mx-net.tx)/net.scale,y:(my-net.ty)/net.scale};}
function hit(mx,my){const w=toWorld(mx,my);return net.nodes.find(n=>{const dx=n.x-w.x,dy=n.y-w.y;return dx*dx+dy*dy<(n.r+4)**2;});}
cv.addEventListener('mousedown',e=>{const r=cv.getBoundingClientRect();const n=hit(e.clientX-r.left,e.clientY-r.top);
  if(n){net.dragn=n;}else{net.drag={x:e.clientX,y:e.clientY,tx:net.tx,ty:net.ty};}});
cv.addEventListener('mousemove',e=>{const r=cv.getBoundingClientRect();const mx=e.clientX-r.left,my=e.clientY-r.top;
  if(net.dragn){const w=toWorld(mx,my);net.dragn.x=w.x;net.dragn.y=w.y;net.dragn.vx=0;net.dragn.vy=0;}
  else if(net.drag){net.tx=net.drag.tx+(e.clientX-net.drag.x);net.ty=net.drag.ty+(e.clientY-net.drag.y);}
  else{const n=hit(mx,my); if(n){tip.style.opacity=1;tip.style.left=(mx+12)+'px';tip.style.top=(my+12)+'px';tip.textContent=n.name+' · '+({g:'gene',d:'condition',p:'org'}[n.t]);cv.style.cursor='pointer';}else{tip.style.opacity=0;cv.style.cursor=net.drag?'grabbing':'grab';}}});
window.addEventListener('mouseup',e=>{if(net.dragn){const r=cv.getBoundingClientRect();const n=hit(e.clientX-r.left,e.clientY-r.top);if(n===net.dragn&&Math.abs(net.dragn.vx)<1){centerNode(net.dragn.name);}}net.dragn=null;net.drag=null;});
cv.addEventListener('wheel',e=>{e.preventDefault();const f=e.deltaY<0?1.1:0.9;const r=cv.getBoundingClientRect();const mx=e.clientX-r.left,my=e.clientY-r.top;
  net.tx=mx-(mx-net.tx)*f;net.ty=my-(my-net.ty)*f;net.scale*=f;},{passive:false});
// search + community list
const nq=document.getElementById('nq'),nres=document.getElementById('nresults');
nq.addEventListener('input',()=>{const f=nq.value.trim().toLowerCase();nres.innerHTML='';if(f.length<2)return;
  GRAPH.nodes.filter(n=>n.name.toLowerCase().includes(f)).slice(0,20).forEach(n=>{
    const d=document.createElement('div');d.className='comitem';d.innerHTML=`<b>${esc(n.name)}</b> <span style="color:#8c83a8">${{g:'gene',d:'condition',p:'org'}[n.t]}</span>`;
    d.onclick=()=>{centerNode(n.name);nq.value='';nres.innerHTML='';};nres.appendChild(d);});});
const comlist=document.getElementById('comlist');
topComs.forEach(c=>{const d=document.createElement('div');d.className='comitem';d.dataset.c=c.id;
  d.innerHTML=`<b>Community ${c.id}</b> · ${c.size} members`;d.onclick=()=>browseCommunity(c.id);comlist.appendChild(d);});
tick();

/* ---------- MATURITY model mockup ---------- */
const stages5=document.getElementById('stages5');
MM.stages.forEach(s=>{const d=document.createElement('div');d.className='stcard';d.style.background=SC[s.id];
  d.innerHTML=`<div class="sn">${s.id}. ${s.name}</div><div class="sd">${esc(s.blurb)}</div>`;stages5.appendChild(d);});
const matgrid=document.getElementById('matgrid');
const hdr=document.createElement('div');hdr.className='hdrrow';
hdr.innerHTML='<div>Track</div>'+MM.stages.map(s=>`<div>Stage ${s.id}</div>`).join('');matgrid.appendChild(hdr);
MM.tracks.forEach(trk=>{const row=document.createElement('div');row.className='matrow';
  row.innerHTML=`<div class="trkhead">${esc(trk.name)}${trk.north_star?'<small>north star</small>':''}</div>`;
  trk.stages.forEach(st=>{const c=document.createElement('div');c.className='cell';
    c.innerHTML=`<div class="cl">${esc(st.label)}</div><div class="cq">${esc(st.q[0])}</div>`;
    c.onclick=()=>showCell(trk,st);row.appendChild(c);});
  matgrid.appendChild(row);});
function showCell(trk,st){
  document.getElementById('mpanel').innerHTML=`
    <button class="close" onclick="document.getElementById('mdetail').classList.remove('show')">×</button>
    <h3>${esc(st.label)}</h3><div class="mtrk">${esc(trk.name)} · Stage ${st.s}</div>
    <div class="blk"><h4>Questions to ask</h4><ul>${st.q.map(q=>`<li>${esc(q)}</li>`).join('')}</ul></div>
    <div class="blk"><h4>Needs support with</h4><p style="margin:0;font-size:14px">${esc(st.needs)}</p></div>
    <div class="blk"><h4>How the network helps</h4><ul>${st.help.map(h=>`<li>${esc(h)}</li>`).join('')}</ul></div>
    <a class="btn" href="../self-assessment.html">Find my stage →</a>`;
  document.getElementById('mdetail').classList.add('show');
}
</script></body></html>
